  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).   - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.  ### 2. Pet Listings Page - **Page Title**: Available Pets - **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options. - **Elements**:   - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.   - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.   - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).   - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 3. Pet Details Page - **Page Title**: Pet Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet. - **Elements**:   - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.   - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.   - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.   - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.   - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.   - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.  ### 4. Add Pet Page - **Page Title**: Add New Pet - **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption. - **Elements**:   - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.   - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.   - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).   - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.   - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").   - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).   - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).   - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.   - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 5. Adoption Application Page - **Page Title**: Adoption Application - **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications. - **Elements**:   - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.   - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.   - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.   - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).   - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.   - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.   - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.  ### 6. My Applications Page - **Page Title**: My Applications - **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user. - **Elements**:   - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.   - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).   - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Favorites Page - **Page Title**: My Favorites - **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites. - **Elements**:   - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.   - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Messages Page - **Page Title**: Messages - **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters. - **Elements**:   - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.   - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.   - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.   - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 9. User Profile Page - **Page Title**: My Profile - **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.   - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).   - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.   - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 10. Admin Panel Page - **Page Title**: Admin Panel - **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets. - **Elements**:   - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.   - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.   - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|email|phone|address   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City   admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave   jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town   ```  ### 2. Pet Data - **File Name**: `pets.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15   2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20   3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01   ```  ### 3. Adoption Applications Data - **File Name**: `applications.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10   2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05   ```  ### 4. Favorites Data - **File Name**: `favorites.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|pet_id|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|2024-11-01   john_doe|3|2024-11-05   jane_smith|2|2024-10-25   ```  ### 5. Messages Data - **File Name**: `messages.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true   2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false   ```  ### 6. Adoption History Data - **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1   ```  ### 7. Shelters Data - **File Name**: `shelters.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   shelter_id|name|address|phone|email   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com   2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org   ```  All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

Backend Design\n\n### 1.1 Overview\nThis backend is designed using Flask. It manages user data, pets data, adoption applications, favorites, messages, shelters as per the requirements. The backend provides routes for each page plus API routes for data handling. All data is stored in text files with pipe (`|`) delimiters.\n\n### 1.2 Routes Definition\n\n| Route Path                  | Function Name         | HTTP Method | Rendered Template      | Context Variables                                            | Redirects | Notes on POST Usage                                                  |\n|-----------------------------|-----------------------|-------------|------------------------|--------------------------------------------------------------|-----------|---------------------------------------------------------------------|\n| `/`                         | home_page             | GET         | `dashboard.html`       | `pets` (list of pet dicts limited to 5)                      | No        | N/A                                                                 |\n| `/pets`                     | pet_listings          | GET, POST   | `pet_listings.html`    | `pets`, `filter_species`, `search_query`                      | No        | POST used for filtering by species and search query                |\n| `/pet/<pet_id>`             | pet_details           | GET         | `pet_details.html`     | `pet` (dict), `favorite_status` (bool)                        | No        | N/A                                                                 |\n| `/pet/new`                  | new_pet               | GET, POST   | `add_pet.html`         | N/A                                                          | Yes (`/`) | POST to add a new pet. Redirects to dashboard on success.          |\n| `/applications/new/<pet_id>`| new_application       | GET, POST   | `new_application.html` | `pet`, `user` (if logged in)                                  | Yes       | POST to submit application. On success redirects to `/applications`|\n| `/applications`             | applications_page     | GET         | `applications.html`    | `applications`, `filter_status`                               | No        | N/A                                                                 |\n| `/favorites`                | favorites_page        | GET         | `favorites.html`       | `favorite_pets`                                              | No        | N/A                                                                 |\n| `/messages`                 | messages_page         | GET, POST   | `messages.html`        | `messages`, `user`                                            | No        | POST to send a new message.                                        |\n| `/profile`                  | profile_page          | GET, POST   | `profile.html`         | `user`                                                       | No        | POST to update profile info.                                       |\n| `/admin`                   | admin_panel           | GET, POST   | `admin_panel.html`     | `pending_applications`, `all_pets`                           | No        | POST to approve/reject applications or manage pets                 |\n\n### 1.3 Route Details\n\n- `/` (Dashboard)\n  - Shows navigation and top 5 available pets.\n  - Context: `pets` list from pets.txt.\n\n- `/pets`\n  - Shows all pets with pagination, filtering by species, search.\n  - POST to accept filter and search inputs.\n\n- `/pet/<pet_id>`\n  - Displays detailed information about a pet.\n  - Context includes pet details, and if user's favorite.\n\n- `/pet/new`\n  - Form for admins to add new pets.\n  - POST creates new pet, validates fields, saves to pets.txt.\n\n- `/applications/new/<pet_id>`\n  - Form for users to submit an adoption application.\n  - POST to create application, save to applications.txt.\n\n- `/applications`\n  - Shows all adoption applications for user/admin with filter.\n\n- `/favorites`\n  - Lists user's favorite pets.\n\n- `/messages`\n  - Shows messaging interface. POST sends message.\n\n- `/profile`\n  - Allows user profile updates.\n\n- `/admin`\n  - Admin panel to approve applications, manage pets.\n\n## 2. Frontend Design\n\n### 2.1 Template Files\n\n- `dashboard.html`\n- `pet_listings.html`\n- `pet_details.html`\n- `add_pet.html`\n- `new_application.html`\n- `applications.html`\n- `favorites.html`\n- `messages.html`\n- `profile.html`\n- `admin_panel.html`\n\n### 2.2 Template Elements with IDs and Types\n\n| Element ID              | Type       | Description/Usage                                        |\n|-------------------------|------------|----------------------------------------------------------|\n| `dashboard-page`        | div        | Container for dashboard page                              |\n| `browse-pets-button`    | button     | Navigate to pet listings                                  |\n| `930324rjqgo6k3rzngh`  | button     | Refresh pets list             |\n| `back-to-dashboard`     | button     | Navigate back to dashboard                                |\n| `pet-details-page`      | div        | Container for pet details page                            |\n| `pet-species`           | div        | Displays pet species                                      |\n| `back-to-pets`          | button     | Back to pet listings                                      |\n| `add-pet-page`          | div        | Container for adding pet                                  |\n| `add-pet-form`          | form       | Form for new pet input                                    |\n| `submit-new-pet`        | button     | Submit new pet                                           |\n| `new-application-page`  | div        | Container for new adoption application                    |\n| `application-form`      | form       | Form for submitting adoption application                  |\n| `submit-application`    | button     | Submit adoption application                               |\n| `applications-page`     | div        | Container for listing applications                        |\n| `applications-table`    | table      | Table    | List all pets with management options                    |\n\n### 2.3 Jinja2 usage\n- Use `url_for` for all button and link hrefs.\n- Context variables passed from backend used via Jinja2 syntax Summary\n- Backend and frontend designed to support all pages and functionality.\n- Clear mapping between routes, frontend templates, and data files.\n- Use of Flask's template rendering and context passing detailed.\n- Data file formats and sample data specified to support backend.\n\n---\n\n(This specification enables seamless parallel development of backend and frontend with clear expectations for data interchange.)"})

User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|email|phone|address   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City   admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave   jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town   ```  ### 2. Pet Data - **File Name**: `pets.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15   2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20   3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01   ```  ### 3. Adoption Applications Data - **File Name**: `applications.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10   2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05   ```  ### 4. Favorites Data - **File Name**: `favorites.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|pet_id|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|2024-11-01   john_doe|3|2024-11-05   jane_smith|2|2024-10-25   ```  ### 5. Messages Data - **File Name**: `messages.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true   2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false   ```  ### 6. Adoption History Data - **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1   ```  ### 7. Shelters Data - **File Name**: `shelters.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   shelter_id|name|address|phone|email   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com   2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org   ```  All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).
  - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.

### 2. Pet Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Available Pets
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.
  - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Pet Details Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.
  - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.
  - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.
  - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.
  - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.

### 4. Add Pet Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Pet
- **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.
  - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.
  - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").
  - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).
  - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).
  - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.
  - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Adoption Application Page
- **Page Title**: Adoption Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.
  - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.
  - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).
  - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.
  - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.

### 6. My Applications Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.
  - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorites
- **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Messages Page
- **Page Title**: Messages
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.
  - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.
  - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.
  - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.
  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Admin Panel Page
- **Page Title**: Admin Panel
- **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.
  - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.
  - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email|phone|address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City
  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave
  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town
  ```

### 2. Pet Data
- **File Name**: `pets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15
  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20
  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01
  ```

### 3. Adoption Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10
  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05
  ```

### 4. Favorites Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|pet_id|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01
  john_doe|3|2024-11-05
  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25
  ```

### 5. Messages Data
- **File Name**: `messages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true
  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false
  ```

### 6. Adoption History Data
- **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1
  ```

### 7. Shelters Data
- **File Name**: `shelters.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

  [user_task_description] # Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application  ## 1. Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).   - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.  ### 2. Pet Listings Page - **Page Title**: Available Pets - **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options. - **Elements**:   - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.   - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.   - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).   - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 3. Pet Details Page - **Page Title**: Pet Details - **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet. - **Elements**:   - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.   - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.   - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.   - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.   - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.   - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.  ### 4. Add Pet Page - **Page Title**: Add New Pet - **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption. - **Elements**:   - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.   - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.   - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).   - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.   - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").   - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).   - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).   - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.   - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 5. Adoption Application Page - **Page Title**: Adoption Application - **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications. - **Elements**:   - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.   - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.   - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.   - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).   - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.   - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.   - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.  ### 6. My Applications Page - **Page Title**: My Applications - **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user. - **Elements**:   - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.   - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).   - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Favorites Page - **Page Title**: My Favorites - **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites. - **Elements**:   - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.   - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 8. Messages Page - **Page Title**: Messages - **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters. - **Elements**:   - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.   - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.   - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.   - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 9. User Profile Page - **Page Title**: My Profile - **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information. - **Elements**:   - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.   - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).   - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.   - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 10. Admin Panel Page - **Page Title**: Admin Panel - **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets. - **Elements**:   - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.   - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.   - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|email|phone|address   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City   admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave   jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town   ```  ### 2. Pet Data - **File Name**: `pets.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15   2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20   3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01   ```  ### 3. Adoption Applications Data - **File Name**: `applications.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10   2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05   ```  ### 4. Favorites Data - **File Name**: `favorites.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|pet_id|date_added   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|2024-11-01   john_doe|3|2024-11-05   jane_smith|2|2024-10-25   ```  ### 5. Messages Data - **File Name**: `messages.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true   2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false   ```  ### 6. Adoption History Data - **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1   ```  ### 7. Shelters Data - **File Name**: `shelters.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   shelter_id|name|address|phone|email   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com   2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org   ```  All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).
  - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.

### 2. Pet Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Available Pets
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.
  - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Pet Details Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.
  - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.
  - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.
  - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.
  - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.

### 4. Add Pet Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Pet
- **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.
  - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.
  - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").
  - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).
  - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).
  - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.
  - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Adoption Application Page
- **Page Title**: Adoption Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.
  - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.
  - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).
  - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.
  - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.

### 6. My Applications Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.
  - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorites
- **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Messages Page
- **Page Title**: Messages
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.
  - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.
  - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.
  - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.
  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Admin Panel Page
- **Page Title**: Admin Panel
- **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.
  - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.
  - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email|phone|address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City
  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave
  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town
  ```

### 2. Pet Data
- **File Name**: `pets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15
  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20
  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01
  ```

### 3. Adoption Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10
  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05
  ```

### 4. Favorites Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|pet_id|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01
  john_doe|3|2024-11-05
  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25
  ```

### 5. Messages Data
- **File Name**: `messages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true
  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false
  ```

### 6. Adoption History Data
- **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1
  ```

### 7. Shelters Data
- **File Name**: `shelters.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).
  - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.

### 2. Pet Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Available Pets
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.
  - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Pet Details Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.
  - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.
  - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.
  - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.
  - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.

### 4. Add Pet Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Pet
- **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.
  - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.
  - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").
  - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).
  - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).
  - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.
  - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Adoption Application Page
- **Page Title**: Adoption Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.
  - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.
  - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).
  - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.
  - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.

### 6. My Applications Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.
  - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorites
- **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Messages Page
- **Page Title**: Messages
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.
  - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.
  - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.
  - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.
  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Admin Panel Page
- **Page Title**: Admin Panel
- **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.
  - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.
  - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email|phone|address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City
  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave
  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town
  ```

### 2. Pet Data
- **File Name**: `pets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15
  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20
  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01
  ```

### 3. Adoption Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10
  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05
  ```

### 4. Favorites Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|pet_id|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01
  john_doe|3|2024-11-05
  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25
  ```

### 5. Messages Data
- **File Name**: `messages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true
  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false
  ```

### 6. Adoption History Data
- **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1
  ```

### 7. Shelters Data
- **File Name**: `shelters.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Requirements Document for 'PetAdoptionCenter' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'PetAdoptionCenter' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to browse available pets for adoption, submit adoption applications, manage favorites, and communicate with shelters. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'PetAdoptionCenter' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' web application will consist of the following ten pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying featured pets, recent activities, and navigation to other functionalities.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: featured-pets** - Type: Div - Display of featured pets available for adoption (limit 5).
  - **ID: browse-pets-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to pet listings page.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to refresh dashboard.

### 2. Pet Listings Page
- **Page Title**: Available Pets
- **Overview**: A page displaying all available pets with filtering and search options.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-listings-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet listings page.
  - **ID: search-input** - Type: Input - Field to search pets by name.
  - **ID: filter-species** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by species (All, Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying pet cards with photo, name, species, and age.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Pet Details Page
- **Page Title**: Pet Details
- **Overview**: A page displaying detailed information about a specific pet.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: pet-details-page** - Type: Div - Container for the pet details page.
  - **ID: pet-name** - Type: H1 - Display pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species** - Type: Div - Display pet species.
  - **ID: pet-description** - Type: Div - Display detailed description about the pet.
  - **ID: adopt-button** - Type: Button - Button to start adoption application process.
  - **ID: back-to-listings** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet listings.

### 4. Add Pet Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Pet
- **Overview**: A page for shelter administrators to add new pets for adoption.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-pet-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add pet page.
  - **ID: pet-name-input** - Type: Input - Field to input pet name.
  - **ID: pet-species-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select species (Dog, Cat, Bird, Rabbit, Other).
  - **ID: pet-breed-input** - Type: Input - Field to input breed.
  - **ID: pet-age-input** - Type: Input - Field to input age (e.g., "2 years").
  - **ID: pet-gender-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select gender (Male, Female).
  - **ID: pet-size-input** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select size (Small, Medium, Large).
  - **ID: pet-description-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to input detailed description.
  - **ID: submit-pet-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit new pet listing.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 5. Adoption Application Page
- **Page Title**: Adoption Application
- **Overview**: A page for users to submit adoption applications.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: application-page** - Type: Div - Container for the application page.
  - **ID: applicant-name** - Type: Input - Field to input applicant's full name.
  - **ID: applicant-phone** - Type: Input - Field to input phone number.
  - **ID: housing-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select housing type (House, Apartment, Condo, Other).
  - **ID: reason** - Type: Textarea - Field to explain why they want to adopt this pet.
  - **ID: submit-application-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit application.
  - **ID: back-to-pet** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to pet details.

### 6. My Applications Page
- **Page Title**: My Applications
- **Overview**: A page displaying all adoption applications submitted by the user.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: my-applications-page** - Type: Div - Container for the my applications page.
  - **ID: filter-status** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to filter by status (All, Pending, Approved, Rejected).
  - **ID: applications-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying applications with pet name, date, status, and actions.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Favorites Page
- **Page Title**: My Favorites
- **Overview**: A page displaying all pets the user has saved as favorites.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: favorites-page** - Type: Div - Container for the favorites page.
  - **ID: favorites-grid** - Type: Div - Grid displaying favorite pet cards.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 8. Messages Page
- **Page Title**: Messages
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and send messages to shelters.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: messages-page** - Type: Div - Container for the messages page.
  - **ID: conversation-list** - Type: Div - List of message conversations.
  - **ID: message-input** - Type: Textarea - Field to compose new message.
  - **ID: send-message-button** - Type: Button - Button to send message.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 9. User Profile Page
- **Page Title**: My Profile
- **Overview**: A page for users to view and edit their profile information.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: profile-page** - Type: Div - Container for the profile page.
  - **ID: profile-username** - Type: Div - Display username (not editable).
  - **ID: profile-email** - Type: Input - Field to update email.
  - **ID: update-profile-button** - Type: Button - Button to save profile changes.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 10. Admin Panel Page
- **Page Title**: Admin Panel
- **Overview**: A page for administrators to manage applications and pets.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: admin-panel-page** - Type: Div - Container for the admin panel page.
  - **ID: pending-applications** - Type: Div - List of pending adoption applications.
  - **ID: all-pets-list** - Type: Div - List of all pets with edit/delete options.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'PetAdoptionCenter' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email|phone|address
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City
  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave
  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town
  ```

### 2. Pet Data
- **File Name**: `pets.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15
  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20
  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01
  ```

### 3. Adoption Applications Data
- **File Name**: `applications.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10
  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05
  ```

### 4. Favorites Data
- **File Name**: `favorites.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|pet_id|date_added
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01
  john_doe|3|2024-11-05
  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25
  ```

### 5. Messages Data
- **File Name**: `messages.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true
  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false
  ```

### 6. Adoption History Data
- **File Name**: `adoption_history.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1
  ```

### 7. Shelters Data
- **File Name**: `shelters.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com
  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

redirects to `/dashboard`.\n- Form submission routes use POST method.\n\n---\n\n## 2. HTML Template Specifications (Frontend Focus)\n\n### 2.1 `templates/dashboard.html`\n- **Page Title**: Pet Adoption Dashboard\n- **Main `<h1>`**: Pet Adoption Dashboard\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `dashboard-page` (div)\n  - `featured-pets` (div)\n  - `browse-pets-button` (button)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `browse-pets-button`: `{{ url_for('pet_listings') }}` (click navigates to `/pets`)\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: reloads `/dashboard`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `featured_pets`: list of dicts, each pet dict:\n    - `pet_id` (int)\n    - `name` (str)\n    - `species` (str)\n    - `age` (str)\n    - `photo_url` (str, optional)\n\n---\n\n### 2.2 `templates/pet_listings.html`\n- **Page Title**: Available Pets\n- **Main `<h1>`**: Available Pets\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `pet-listings-page` (div)\n  - `search-input` (input)\n  - `filter-species` (select)\n  - `pet-grid` (div)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: `{{ url_for('dashboard') }}`\n  - Clicking pet card navigates to `{{ url_for('pet_details', pet_id=pet.pet_id) }}`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `pets`: list of dicts; each dict:\n    - `pet_id` (int)\n    - `name` (str)\n    - `species` (str)\n    - `age` (str)\n    - `photo_url` (str, optional)\n  - `filter_species`: str\n  - `search_query`: str\n\n---\n\n### 2.3 `templates/pet_details.html`\n- **Page Title**: Pet Details\n- **Main `<h1>`**: `{{ pet.name }}`\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `pet-details-page` (div)\n  - `pet-name` (h1)\n  - `pet-species` (div)\n  - `pet-description` (div)\n  - `adopt-button` (button)\n  - `back-to-listings` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `adopt-button`: `{{ url_for('new_application', pet_id=pet.pet_id) }}`\n  - `back-to-listings`: `{{ url_for('pet_listings') }}`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `pet`: dict with keys:\n    - `pet_id` (int)\n    - `name` (str)\n    - `species` (str)\n    - `breed` (str)\n    - `age` (str)\n    - `gender` (str)\n    - `size` (str)\n    - `description` (str)\n    - `shelter_id` (int)\n    - `status` (str)\n    - `date_added` (str)\n  - `is_favorite`: bool\n\n---\n\n### 2.4 `templates/add_pet.html`\n- **Page Title**: Add New Pet\n- **Main `<h1>`**: Add New Pet\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `add-pet-page` (div)\n  - `pet-name-input` (input)\n  - `pet-species-input` (select)\n  - `pet-breed-input` (input)\n  - `pet-age-input` (input)\n  - `pet-gender-input` (select)\n  - `pet-size-input` (select)\n  - `pet-description-input` (textarea)\n  - `submit-pet-button` (button)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: `{{ url_for('dashboard') }}`\n- **Context Variables:** None (empty form)\n\n---\n\n### 2.5 `templates/application.html`\n- **Page Title**: Adoption Application\n- **Main `<h1>`**: Adoption Application\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `application-page` (div)\n  - `applicant-name` (input)\n  - `applicant-phone` (input)\n  - `housing-type` (select)\n  - `reason` (textarea)\n  - `submit-application-button` (button)\n  - `back-to-pet` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-pet`: `{{ url_for('pet_details', pet_id=pet.pet_id) }}`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `pet`: dict (same structure as in pet_details.html)\n\n---\n\n### 2.6 `templates/my_applications.html`\n- **Page Title**: My Applications\n- **Main `<h1>`**: My Applications\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `my-applications-page` (div)\n  - `filter-status` (select)\n  - `applications-table` (table)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: `{{ url_for('dashboard') }}`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `applications`: list of dicts, each with:\n    - `application_id` (int)\n    - `pet_name` (str)\n    - `date_submitted` (str)\n    - `status` (str)\n  - `filter_status`: str\n\n---\n\n### 2.7 `templates/favorites.html`\n- **Page Title**: My Favorites\n- **Main `<h1>`**: My Favorites\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `favorites-page` (div)\n  - `favorites-grid` (div)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: `{{ url_for('dashboard') }}`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `favorite_pets`: list of dicts with pet details\n\n---\n\n### 2.8 `templates/messages.html`\n- **Page Title**: Messages\n- **Main `<h1>`**: Messages\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `messages-page` (div)\n  - `conversation-list` (div)\n  - `message-input` (textarea)\n  - `send-message-button` (button)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: `{{ url_for('dashboard') }}`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `messages`: list of dicts\n\n---\n\n### 2.9 `templates/profile.html`\n- **Page Title**: My Profile\n- **Main `<h1>`**: My Profile\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `profile-page` (div)\n  - `profile-username` (div)\n  - `profile-email` (input)\n  - `update-profile-button` (button)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: `{{ url_for('dashboard') }}`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `user`: dict with `username` (str), `email` (str), `phone` (str), `address` (str)\n\n---\n\n### 2.10 `templates/admin_panel.html`\n- **Page Title**: Admin Panel\n- **Main `<h1>`**: Admin Panel\n- **Element IDs & Types:**\n  - `admin-panel-page` (div)\n  - `pending-applications` (div)\n  - `all-pets-list` (div)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard`: `{{ url_for('dashboard') }}`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `pending_applications`: list of dicts\n  - `all_pets`: list of dicts\n\n---\n\n## 3. Data File Schemas (Backend Focus)\n\n### 3.1 `users.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  username|email|phone|address\n  ```\n- **Description:** Stores registered users' information.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  john_doe|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St, City\n  admin_user|admin@shelter.com|555-0000|456 Shelter Ave\n  jane_smith|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak Rd, Town\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### 3.2 `pets.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  pet_id|name|species|breed|age|gender|size|description|shelter_id|status|date_added\n  ```\n- **Description:** Stores details of pets available for adoption or in shelter.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|Buddy|Dog|Golden Retriever|3 years|Male|Large|Friendly and energetic dog who loves to play fetch.|1|Available|2024-10-15\n  2|Whiskers|Cat|Siamese|2 years|Female|Small|Calm and affectionate cat, great with children.|1|Pending|2024-10-20\n  3|Charlie|Dog|Beagle|5 years|Male|Medium|Gentle senior dog looking for a quiet home.|2|Available|2024-11-01\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### 3.3 `applications.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  application_id|username|pet_id|applicant_name|phone|address|housing_type|has_yard|other_pets|experience|reason|status|date_submitted\n  ```\n- **Description:** Stores adoption application data.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|john_doe|1|John Doe|555-1234|123 Main St|House|Yes|One cat|5 years with dogs|Looking for a companion for hiking|Pending|2024-11-10\n  2|jane_smith|2|Jane Smith|555-5678|789 Oak Rd|Apartment|No|None|First time pet owner|Always wanted a cat|Approved|2024-11-05\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### 3.4 `favorites.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  username|pet_id|date_added\n  ```\n- **Description:** Tracks pets favorited by users.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  john_doe|1|2024-11-01\n  john_doe|3|2024-11-05\n  jane_smith|2|2024-10-25\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### 3.5 `messages.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  message_id|sender_username|recipient_username|subject|content|timestamp|is_read\n  ```\n- **Description:** Stores messages between users and shelters.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|john_doe|admin_user|Question about Buddy|Is Buddy good with other dogs?|2024-11-10 14:30:00|true\n  2|admin_user|john_doe|Re: Question about Buddy|Yes, Buddy is great with other dogs!|2024-11-10 15:00:00|false\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### 3.6 `adoption_history.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  history_id|username|pet_id|pet_name|adoption_date|shelter_id\n  ```\n- **Description:** Records past adoptions.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|jane_smith|2|Whiskers|2024-11-15|1\n  ```\n\n---\n\n### 3.7 `shelters.txt`\n- **Format:**\n  ```\n  shelter_id|name|address|phone|email\n  ```\n- **Description:** Contains shelter information.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  ```\n  1|Happy Paws Shelter|100 Shelter Lane, City|555-1000|contact@happypaws.com\n  2|Second Chance Animals|200 Rescue Road, Town|555-2000|info@secondchance.org\n  ```\n\n---\n\n# End of Design Specification\n\nThis file fully describes the Flask routes, HTML templates, and backend data file schemas enabling independent backend and frontend development."})
